(hasHistory) {\n382\t      mainContent.classList.add('has-history');\n383\t    } else {\n384\t      mainContent.classList.remove('has-history');\n385\t    }\n386\t  }\n387\t};\n388\t\n389\t// Transcript display functions\n390\tconst showTranscript = () => {\n391\t  const card = document.getElementById('transcript-card');\n392\t  // Only show and switch layout when there's actual content (not empty placeholders)\n393\t  const hasVisibleContent = transcriptMessages.some(msg => msg.content || msg.streaming);\n394\t  if (card && hasVisibleContent) card.classList.add('visible');\n395\t  updateLayoutMode(hasVisibleContent);\n396\t};\n397\t\n398\tconst hideTranscript = () => {\n399\t  const card = document.getElementById('transcript-card');\n400\t  if (card) card.classList.remove('visible');\n401\t  updateLayoutMode(false);\n402\t};\n403\t\n404\tconst clearTranscript = () => {\n405\t  transcriptMessages = [];\n406\t  renderTranscript();\n407\t  updateLayoutMode(false);\n408\t};\n409\t\n410\t// Find message by itemId\n411\tconst findMessageByItemId = (itemId) => {\n412\t  return transcriptMessages.findIndex(msg => msg.itemId === itemId);\n413\t};\n414\t\n415\t// Create placeholder for conversation item (called when item is created - correct order)\n416\tconst createMessagePlaceholder = (itemId, role) => {\n417\t  // Check if already exists\n418\t  if (findMessageByItemId(itemId) !== -1) return;\n419\t  transcriptMessages.push({\n420\t    itemId,\n421\t    role,\n422\t    content: '',\n423\t    timestamp: Date.now(),\n424\t    pending: true  // Mark as waiting for transcription\n425\t  });\n426\t  renderTranscript();\n427\t  showTranscript();\n428\t};\n429\t\n430\t// Update message content by itemId\n431\tconst updateMessageByItemId = (itemId, content, options = {}) => {\n432\t  const index = findMessageByItemId(itemId);\n433\t  if (index !== -1) {\n434\t    transcriptMessages[index].content = content;\n435\t    transcriptMessages[index].pending = false;\n436\t    if (options.streaming !== undefined) {\n437\t      transcriptMessages[index].streaming = options.streaming;\n438\t    }\n439\t    renderTranscript();\n440\t    showTranscript();\n441\t    return index;\n442\t  }\n443\t  return -1;\n444\t};\n445\t\n446\t// Add a tool call message to the transcript\n447\tconst addToolCallMessage = (name, args, callId) => {\n448\t  transcriptMessages.push({\n449\t    role: 'tool',\n450\t    type: 'tool_call',\n451\t    toolName: name,\n452\t    toolArgs: args,\n453\t    callId: callId,\n454\t    status: 'pending',\n455\t    result: null,\n456\t    timestamp: Date.now()\n457\t  });\n458\t  renderTranscript();\n459\t  showTranscript();\n460\t};\n461\t\n462\t// Legacy function for messages without itemId\n463\tconst addTranscriptMessage = (role, content, itemId = null) => {\n464\t  if (itemId) {\n465\t    const index = findMessageByItemId(itemId);\n466\t    if (index !== -1) {\n467\t      // Update existing placeholder\n468\t      transcriptMessages[index].content = content;\n469\t      transcriptMessages[index].pending = false;\n470\t      renderTranscript();\n471\t      showTranscript();\n472\t      return;\n473\t    }\n474\t  }\n475\t  // Fallback: add new message\n476\t  transcriptMessages.push({ role, content, timestamp: Date.now(), itemId });\n477\t  renderTranscript();\n478\t  showTranscript();\n479\t};\n480\t\n481\t// Start a new streaming response (returns index)\n482\tconst startStreamingResponse = (role, itemId = null) => {\n483\t  let index;\n484\t  if (itemId) {\n485\t    index = findMessageByItemId(itemId);\n486\t    if (index !== -1) {\n487\t      // Use existing placeholder\n488\t      transcriptMessages[index].streaming = true;\n489\t      transcriptMessages[index].pending = false;\n490\t    } else {\n491\t      // Create new with itemId\n492\t      index = transcriptMessages.length;\n493\t      transcriptMessages.push({ role, content: '', timestamp: Date.now(), streaming: true, itemId });\n494\t    }\n495\t  } else {\n496\t    index = transcriptMessages.length;\n497\t    transcriptMessages.push({ role, content: '', timestamp: Date.now(), streaming: true });\n498\t  }\n499\t  streamingResponse = { index, content: '', role, itemId };\n500\t  renderTranscript();\n501\t  showTranscript();\n502\t  return index;\n503\t};\n504\t\n505\t// Append to streaming response\n506\tconst appendToStreamingResponse = (delta) => {\n507\t  if (!streamingResponse) return;\n508\t  streamingResponse.content += delta;\n509\t  transcriptMessages[streamingResponse.index].content = streamingResponse.content;\n510\t  renderTranscript(true); // Pass true to indicate streaming update\n511\t};\n512\t\n513\t// Finalize streaming response\n514\tconst finalizeStreamingResponse = (finalContent) => {\n515\t  if (!streamingResponse) return;\n516\t  // Use final content if provided, otherwise keep accumulated content\n517\t  if (finalContent) {\n518\t    transcriptMessages[streamingResponse.index].content = finalContent;\n519\t  }\n520\t  transcriptMessages[streamingResponse.index].streaming = false;\n521\t  streamingResponse = null;\n522\t  renderTranscript();\n523\t};\n524\t\n525\tconst renderTranscript = (isStreamingUpdate = false) => {\n526\t  const container = document.getElementById('transcript-content');\n527\t  if (!container) return;\n528\t\n529\t  if (transcriptMessages.length === 0) {\n530\t    container.innerHTML = '<div class=\"transcript-empty\">Conversation transcript will appear here...</div>';\n531\t    return;\n532\t  }\n533\t\n534\t  // For streaming updates, only update the streaming message's text (much faster)\n535\t  if (isStreamingUpdate && streamingResponse) {\n536\t    const streamingEl = container.querySelector(`[data-idx=\"${streamingResponse.index}\"] .transcript-text`);\n537\t    if (streamingEl) {\n538\t      const msg = transcriptMessages[streamingResponse.index];\n539\t      let contentHtml = msg.content || '';\n540\t      // Simple text for streaming - skip markdown parsing for performance\n541\t      contentHtml = contentHtml.replace(/\\n/g, '<br>');\n542\t      contentHtml += '<span class=\"streaming-cursor\">▋</span>';\n543\t      streamingEl.innerHTML = contentHtml;\n544\t      container.scrollTop = container.scrollHeight;\n545\t      return;\n546\t    }\n547\t  }\n548\t\n549\t  // Full render for new messages or finalization\n550\t  // Filter out pending placeholders with no content (always include tool_call messages)\n551\t  const visibleMessages = transcriptMessages.filter(msg => msg.content || msg.streaming || msg.type === 'tool_call');\n552\t\n553\t  if (visibleMessages.length === 0) {\n554\t    container.innerHTML = '<div class=\"transcript-empty\">Conversation transcript will appear here...</div>';\n555\t    return;\n556\t  }\n557\t\n558\t  const html = visibleMessages.map((msg, idx) => {\n559\t    // Tool call messages — collapsed by default, expand to see request + response\n560\t    if (msg.type === 'tool_call') {\n561\t      let argsFormatted = msg.toolArgs || '';\n562\t      try {\n563\t        argsFormatted = JSON.stringify(JSON.parse(msg.toolArgs), null, 2);\n564\t      } catch (e) { /* keep raw */ }\n565\t\n566\t      const statusClass = msg.status === 'completed' ? 'completed' : 'pending';\n567\t\n568\t      // Response section inside the expandable body\n569\t      let resultHtml = '';\n570\t      if (msg.result) {\n571\t        resultHtml = `\n572\t          <div class=\"tool-call-section\">\n573\t            <div class=\"tool-call-section-label\">Response</div>\n574\t            <pre class=\"tool-call-section-text\">${msg.result}</pre>\n575\t          </div>`;\n576\t      } else if (msg.status === 'pending') {\n577\t        resultHtml = `\n578\t          <div class=\"tool-call-section\">\n579\t            <span class=\"tool-call-loading\">Waiting for result...</span>\n580\t          </div>`;\n581\t      }\n582\t\n583\t      return `\n584\t        <div class=\"transcript-message tool-call\" data-idx=\"${idx}\">\n585\t          <details class=\"tool-call-details\">\n586\t            <summary class=\"tool-call-summary\">\n587\t              <span class=\"tool-call-icon\">🔧</span>\n588\t              <span class=\"tool-call-name\">${msg.toolName}</span>\n589\t              <span class=\"tool-call-status ${statusClass}\">${msg.status}</span>\n590\t            </summary>\n591\t            <div class=\"tool-call-body\">\n592\t              <div class=\"tool-call-section\">\n593\t                <div class=\"tool-call-section-label\">Request</div>\n594\t                <pre class=\"tool-call-section-text\">${argsFormatted}</pre>\n595\t              </div>\n596\t              ${resultHtml}\n597\t            </div>\n598\t          </details>\n599\t        </div>\n600\t      `;\n601\t    }\n602\t\n603\t    const roleClass = msg.role === 'user' ? 'user' : 'assistant';\n604\t    const roleLabel = msg.role === 'user' ? 'You' : 'DUCK-E';\n605\t    const streamingClass = msg.streaming ? ' streaming' : '';\n606\t\n607\t    // Parse markdown if marked is available (skip for empty streaming)\n608\t    let contentHtml = msg.content || '';\n609\t    if (contentHtml && typeof marked !== 'undefined' && !msg.streaming) {\n610\t      try {\n611\t        contentHtml = marked.parse(msg.content);\n612\t      } catch (e) {\n613\t        console.warn('Markdown parsing failed:', e);\n614\t        contentHtml = msg.content.replace(/\\n/g, '<br>');\n615\t      }\n616\t    } else if (contentHtml) {\n617\t      contentHtml = msg.content.replace(/\\n/g, '<br>');\n618\t    }\n619\t\n620\t    // Show cursor for streaming messages\n621\t    if (msg.streaming) {\n622\t      contentHtml += '<span class=\"streaming-cursor\">▋</span>';\n623\t    }\n624\t\n625\t    return `\n626\t      <div class=\"transcript-message ${roleClass}${streamingClass}\" data-idx=\"${idx}\">\n627\t        <div class=\"transcript-label\">${roleLabel}</div>\n628\t        <div class=\"transcript-text\">${contentHtml}</div>\n629\t      </div>\n630\t    `;\n631\t  }).join('');\n632\t\n633\t  container.innerHTML = html;\n634\t\n635\t  // Auto-scroll to bottom\n636\t  container.scrollTop = container.scrollHeight;\n637\t};\n638\t\n639\t// Handle incoming messages from WebRTC for transcript\n640\tconst handleWebRTCMessage = (event) => {\n641\t  try {\n642\t    // event now has { data: string, message: object } from our modified ag2client\n643\t    const data = event.message || (typeof event.data === 'string' ? JSON.parse(event.data) : event.data);\n644\t\n645\t    // Perf telemetry hooks\n646\t    if (data.type === 'input_audio_buffer.speech_started') {\n647\t      perfReset();\n648\t      perfTimeline.speechStarted = perfTs();\n649\t      console.log(`[DUCK-E Perf] speech_started ts=${perfTimeline.speechStarted.toFixed(0)}ms`);\n650\t    } else if (data.type === (perfTimeline.speechStarted ?? perfTimeline.speechStopped);\n654\t        console.log(`[DUCK-E Perf] speech_stopped  speech_dur=${delta.toFixed(0)}ms`);\n655\t      }\n656\t    } else if (data.type perfTimeline.speechStopped ?? perfTimeline.speechStarted;\n660\t        const delta = start != null ? perfTimeline.transcriptionDone - start : null;\n661\t        console.log(`[DUCK-E Perf] transcription_done  transcription_dur=${delta != null ? delta.toFixed(0) : '?'}ms`);\n662\t      }\n663\t    } else if (data.type === 'response.created') {\n664\t      if (!perfTimeline) 'response.output_item.done') {\n674\t      if (perfTimeline && data.item?.type === 'function_call') {\n675\t        const callId = data.item.call_id;\n676\t        if (perfTimeline.toolCalls[callId]) {\n677\t          perfTimeline.toolCalls[callId].resultReceived = perfTs();\n678\t          const dur = perfTimeline.toolCalls[callId].resultReceived - perfTimeline.toolCalls[callId].dispatched;\n679\t          console.log(`[DUCK-E Perf] tool_result_received  tool=${data.item.name} call_id=${callId} dur=${dur.toFixed(0)}ms`);\n680\t        }\n681\t      }\n682\t    } else if (data.type === 'response.done') {\n683\t      if (perfTimeline) {\n684\t        perfTimeline.responseDone = perfTs();\n685\t        perfLogSummary();\n686\t      }\n687\t    }\n688\t\n689\t    // Log message types for debugging (can be removed later)\n690\t    if (data.type) {\n691\t      console.log('WebRTC message type:', data.type);\n692\t    }\n693\t\n694\t    // Handle different message types from OpenAI Realtime API\n695\t\n696\t    // Conversation item created - create placeholder in correct order\n697\t    if (data.type === 'conversation.item.created') createMessagePlaceholder(item.id, item.role);\n702\t      }\n703\t    }\n704\t    // User's speech transcription completed - update placeholder by item_id\n705\t    else if (data.type === addTranscriptMessage('assistant', data.transcript, itemId);\n744\t      }\n745\t    }\n746\t    // Assistant's text response DELTA (streaming)\n747\t    else if (data.type === 'response.text.delta') const output = data.item.output;\n782\t      console.log('Tool result received for call_id:', callId, output);\n783\t      const idx = transcriptMessages.findIndex(\n784\t        msg => msg.type === }\n791\t    // Output item done - mark matching tool call as completed\n792\t    else if (data.type === 'response.output_item.done') {\n793\t      const item = data.item;\n794\t      if (item && type: 'ducke.turn_done',\n819\t            user_text: currentTurnUserTranscript,\n820\t            assistant_text: currentTurnAssistantTranscript,\n821\t          }));\n822\t          currentTurnAssistantTranscript = ''; // Reset for next response in same turn\n823\t        }\n824\t      }\n825\t    }\n826\t    // OpenAI Realtime API error — surface to transcript so it's visible\n827\t    else if (data.type === 'error') {\n828\t      const errMsg = data.error?.message || JSON.stringify(data.error) || 'Unknown error';\n829\t      console.error('[DUCK-E] Realtime API (web_search, memory extraction via gpt-5.4-nano)\n842\t    else if (data.type === 'ducke.backend_cost') {\n843\t      if (!sessionCost.startTime) sessionCost.startTime = Date.now();\n844\t      sessionCost.backendInputTokens  += data.input_tokens  || 0;\n845\t      sessionCost.backendOutputTokens += data.output_tokens || 0;\n846\t      refreshCostDisplay();\n847\t    }\n848\t  } catch (e) {\n849\t    console.error('Error handling WebRTC message:', e);\n850\t  }\n851\t};\n852\t\n853\t// Function to update the UI elements based on connection status.\n854\tconst updateUI = (status) => It provides voice-first interaction with tools for weather, web search, web fetch, memory, and voice changing.\n\n## Architecture\n\n```\nBrowser (WebRTC) → WebSocket → FastAPI → OpenAI Realtime API\n                                      ↓\n                                 Tools (weather/search/memory/fetch)\n```\n\n### Key Components\n\n| File | Purpose |\n|------|---------|\n| `app/main.py` | FastAPI app, WebSocket endpoint `/session`, tool handlers |\n| `app/realtime_session.py` | Custom RealtimeSession (replaced AG2 RealtimeAgent) |\n| `app/memory.py` | UserMemoryStore for per-user facts (JSON file store) |\n| `app/config.py` | OpenAI config generation (`get_realtime_config()`) |\n| `app/website_files/static/main.js` | Frontend: WebRTC, cost tracking, transcript rendering |\n| `app/website_files/static/ag2client.js` | WebRTC+WebSocket bridge (originally AG2, now compatible) |\n| `app/middleware/` | Rate limiting, cost protection, security headers |\n\n## Development\n\n### Running locally\n\n```bash\n# Install deps\npip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# Set required env vars in .env:\n# OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-...\n# WEATHER_API_KEY=...\n\n# Run dev server\nuvicorn app.main:app --reload --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\n```\n\n### Docker\n\n```bash\ndocker build -t duck-e:latest .\ndocker run -p 8000:8000 -e OPENAI_API_KEY=... -e WEATHER_API_KEY=... duck-e:latest\n```\n\n## Important Patterns\n\n### Tool Registration\n\nTools are registered in `main.py` via `session.register_tool()`:\n\n```python\nsession.register_tool(\n    name=\"get_current_weather\",\n    description=\"Get current weather for a location\",\n    handler=get_current_weather,\n    parameters={...}  # OpenAI JSON schema\n)\n```\n\n### WebSocket Message Flow\n\n1. Client connects → `RealtimeSession.run()` accepts WebSocket\n2. Server fetches ephemeral key from `/v1/realtime/sessions`\n3. Server sends `ag2.init` message with config (ephemeral key only, never real API key)\n4. Client establishes WebRTC data channel\n5. Tool calls flow: `response.function_call_arguments.done` → execute → `conversation.item.create`\n\n### Cost Tracking\n\n- Server-side: `CostProtectionMiddleware` limits per-session spend ($5 default)\n- Client-side: `main.js` accumulates usage from `response.done` events, displays hourly estimate\n- Backend API calls (web_search via OpenAI Responses API) tracked separately\n\n### Memory System\n\n- User identity from headers: `x-forwarded-user`, `x-forwarded-email`\n- JSON file store: `/data/memory/{user_hash}.json`\n- Tools: `save_memory(fact)`, `recall_memories()`\n- Memories injected into system message at session start\n\n### Security\n\n- **SSRF protection**: `FetchUrl` validator resolves hostnames, blocks private IPs\n- **Rate limiting**: Per-IP limits via `slowapi`\n- **Input validation**: `LocationInput`, `SearchQuery`, `FetchUrl` validators\n- **CORS**: Origin whitelist in `app.middleware.configure_cors()`\n- **Cost protection**: $5/session hard limit, $100 circuit breaker\n\n## Model Configuration\n\nUses `gpt-realtime-1.5` for voice sessions. Config generated in `app/config.py`:\n\n```python\n{\n    \"model\": \"gpt-realtime-1.5\",\n    \"api_key\": os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\"),\n    \"voice\": \"alloy\",  # changeable via tool\n}\n```\n\n## Testing\n\n```bash\n# Run tests\npytest\n\n# Security tests (92% coverage)\npytest tests/security/\n```\n\n## Deployment\n\n- ArgoCD WorkflowTemplate: `duck-e-build` → Docker image → `ghcr.io/jedarden/duck-e`\n- Production: behind oauth2-proxy or Tailscale auth for header injection\n- Prometheus metrics: `/metrics`\n\n## Common Gotchas\n\n1. **Ephemeral key flow**: Never send real `OPENAI_API_KEY` to client. Only send `client_secret.value` from `/v1/realtime/sessions` response.\n2. **Voice change**: Requires session reinit — `change_voice` tool sends new config, client reconnects WebRTC.\n3. **Memory persistence**: Requires user headers from reverse proxy — won't work in local dev without mocking headers.\n4. **AG2 references**: Code still uses `ag2.init` message type for client compatibility, but backend is custom `RealtimeSession`.\n5. **Cost display resets**: On reconnect, `resetCostState()` called in `main.js` → `connectAudio()`.\n","numLines":129,"startLine":1,"totalLines":129}}}

Summary\n4\t\n5\tDUCK-E is a real-time voice assistant built on:\n6\t- **Backend**: FastAPI (Python) with AG2 (AutoGen) `RealtimeAgent` for orchestrating OpenAI Realtime API sessions\n7\t- autogen.agentchat.realtime_agent import RealtimeAgent` |\n18\t| `app/main.py:288-294` | `RealtimeAgent(name, system_message, llm_config, websocket, logger)` |\n19\t| `app/main.py:314-441` | |\n23\t\n24\t---\n25\t\n26\t## Change 1: Remove AG2 Dependency Entirely\n27\t\n28\t### What AG2 `RealtimeAgent` Actually Does\n29\t\n30\tBy reading `ag2client.js` and tracing the backend, `RealtimeAgent` provides:\n31\t\n32\t1. **Ephemeral key generation** — Calls OpenAI's `/v1/realtime/sessions` to get a short-lived client secret\n33\t2. **Session configuration** — Sends an `ag2.init` message over WebSocket containing the ephemeral key, model name, and init chunks (system message, tool definitions, session config)\n34\t3. **Tool call relay** — Receives `function_call` messages from the WebRTC data channel (forwarded via WebSocket), executes registered Python functions, and sends results back\n35\t4. **WebSocket lifecycle** — Manages accept/close and message routing\n36\t\n37\t### Security Issue: API Key Exposure\n38\t\n39\t**The current design leaks the OpenAI API key to the frontend.** In `ag2client.js`, the ephemeral key flow works correctly (the *ephemeral* client secret is sent to the browser, not the real API key). However, the `RealtimeSession` must ensure:\n40\t\n41\t1. The real `OPENAI_API_KEY` is **never** included in any WebSocket message to the client\n42\t2. Only the ephemeral `client_secret` from `/v1/realtime/sessions` is sent in the init message\n43\t3. The `config` object sent to the client must be stripped of any `api_key` fields before transmission\n44\t\n45\tThe ephemeral key endpoint returns a response like:\n46\t```json\n47\t{\n48\t  \"id\": \"sess_...\",\n49\t  \"client_secret\": {\"value\": \"ek_...\", \"expires_at\": 1234567890},\n50\t  \"model\": \"gpt-realtime-1.5\",\n51\t  ...\n52\t}\n53\t```\n54\t\n55\tOnly `client_secret.value` and `model` should reach the client. The `RealtimeSession` must explicitly construct a sanitized config object rather than forwarding the raw API response.\n56\t\n57\t### Replacement Strategy\n58\t\n59\tReplace `RealtimeAgent` with a custom `RealtimeSession` class (~150 lines) that:\n60\t\n61\t1. Calls `POST https://api.openai.com/v1/realtime/sessions` **server-side** with the real API key to obtain an ephemeral client secret\n62\t2. Constructs a **sanitized** init message containing only the ephemeral key and model — never the real API key\n63\t3. Sends the init message over the WebSocket to the client\n64\t4. Listens for incoming WebSocket messages containing `function_call` / `function_call_output` types\n65\t5. Dispatches tool calls to registered handler functions\n66\t6. Returns results back through the WebSocket → data channel path\n67\t\n68\t### Files to Modify\n69\t\n70\t| File | Change |\n71\t|------|--------|\n72\t| `requirements.txt` | Remove `ag2==0.9.10` |\n73\t| `app/config.py` | Simplify — remove tag-based filtering, just provide `{model, api_key}` dicts directly |\n74\t| `app/main.py` | Replace `RealtimeAgent` import and usage with new `RealtimeSession` class |\n75\t| `app/realtime_session.py` | **NEW** — Custom `RealtimeSession` implementation |\n76\t| `app/website_files/static/ag2client.js` | Rename references from `ag2` to `ducke`, update `ag2.init` → `ducke.init` message type (or keep compatible) |\n77\t\n78\t### Implementation Details for `RealtimeSession`\n79\t\n80\t```python\n81\tclass RealtimeSession:\n82\t    def __init__(self, websocket, model, api_key, system_message, tools, voice=\"alloy\", logger=None):\n83\t        self.websocket = websocket\n84\t        self.model = model\n85\t        self.api_key = api_key\n86\t        self.system_message = system_message\n87\t        self.tools = tools  # List of tool definitions\n88\t        self.tool_handlers = {}  # name -> callable\n89\t        self.voice = voice\n90\t        self.logger = logger\n91\t\n92\t    def register_tool(self, name, description, handler, parameters):\n93\t        \"\"\"Register a tool function (replaces @register_realtime_function)\"\"\"\n94\t        self.tool_handlers[name] = handler\n95\t        self.tools.append({\n96\t            \"type\": \"function\",\n97\t            \"name\": name,\n98\t            \"description\": description,\n99\t            \"parameters\": parameters\n100\t        })\n101\t\n102\t    async def _get_ephemeral_key(self):\n103\t        \"\"\"Call OpenAI /v1/realtime/sessions to get client secret.\n104\t        Returns a SANITIZED config safe for the client — never exposes the real API key.\"\"\"\n105\t        async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:\n106\t            resp = await client.post(\n107\t                \"https://api.openai.com/v1/realtime/sessions\",\n108\t                headers={\n109\t                    \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.api_key}\",\n110\t                    \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"\n111\t                },\n112\t                json={\n113\t                    \"model\": self.model,\n114\t                    \"voice\": self.voice,\n115\t                    \"instructions\": self.system_message,\n116\t                    \"tools\": self.tools,\n117\t                    \"input_audio_transcription\": {\"model\": \"whisper-1\"}\n118\t                }\n119\t            )\n120\t            resp.raise_for_status()\n121\t            data = resp.json()\n122\t\n123\t            # SECURITY: Only return fields the client needs.\n124\t            # Never forward the raw response — it may contain server-side metadata.\n125\t            return {\n126\t                \"client_secret\": data[\"client_secret\"],  # ephemeral key (short-lived)\n127\t                \"model\": data.get(\"model\", self.model),\n128\t            }\n129\t\n130\t    async def run(self):\n131\t        \"\"\"Main session loop — replaces realtime_agent.run()\"\"\"\n132\t        await self.websocket.accept()\n133\t        session_data = await self._get_ephemeral_key()\n134\t\n135\t        # Send init message to client (compatible with ag2client.js)\n136\t        # SECURITY: session_data contains only ephemeral key + model, never the real API key\n137\t        await self.websocket.send_json({\n138\t            \"type\": \"ag2.init\",  # Keep compatible with existing client\n139\t            \"config\": session_data,\n140\t            \"init\": []  # Session config chunks\n141\t        })\n142\t\n143\t        # Listen for tool calls from client\n144\t        try:\n145\t            while True:\n146\t                data = await self.websocket.receive_json()\n147\t                if data.get(\"type\") == \"response.function_call_arguments.done\":\n148\t                    result = await self._handle_tool_call(data)\n149\t                    await self.websocket.send_json(result)\n150\t        except WebSocketDisconnect:\n151\t            pass\n152\t\n153\t    async def _handle_tool_call(self, data):\n154\t        \"\"\"Execute registered tool and return result\"\"\"\n155\t        name = data.get(\"name\")\n156\t        args = json.loads(data.get(\"arguments\", \"{}\"))\n157\t        handler = self.tool_handlers.get(name)\n158\t        if handler:\n159\t            result = handler(**args) if not asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(handler) else await handler(**args)\n160\t            return {\n161\t                \"type\": \"conversation.item.create\",\n162\t                \"item\": {\n163\t                    \"type\": \"function_call_output\",\n164\t                    \"call_id\": data.get(\"call_id\"),\n165\t                    \"output\": str(result)\n166\t                }\n167\t            }\n168\t```\n169\t\n170\t### Migration of Tool Registration\n171\t\n172\t**Before (AG2):**\n173\t```python\n174\t@realtime_agent.register_realtime_function(\n175\t    name=\"get_current_weather\", description=\"Get the current weather\"\n176\t)\n177\tdef get_current_weather(location: Annotated[str, \"city\"]) -> str:\n178\t    ...\n179\t```\n180\t\n181\t**After (Custom):**\n182\t```python\n183\tsession.register_tool(\n184\t    name=\"get_current_weather\",\n185\t    description=\"Get the current weather\",\n186\t    handler=get_current_weather,\n187\t    parameters={\"type\": \"object\", \"properties\": {\"location\": {\"type\": \"string\", \"description\": \"city\"}}, \"required\": [\"location\"]}\n188\t)\n189\t```\n190\t\n191\tOr use a decorator wrapper that mirrors the old API for minimal diff.\n192\t\n193\t---\n194\t\n195\t## Change 2: Replace Model with `gpt-realtime-1.5`\n196\t\n197\t### Files to Modify\n198\t\n199\t| File | Change |\n200\t|------|--------|\n201\t| `app/config.py` | Change `\"model\": \"gpt-realtime\"` → `\"model\": \"gpt-realtime-1.5\"` |\n202\t| `app/realtime_session.py` | Default model parameter = `\"gpt-realtime-1.5\"` |\n203\t\n204\t### Notes\n205\t- The model name is passed to OpenAI's `/v1/realtime/sessions` endpoint and to the WebRTC SDP negotiation URL (`https://api.openai.com/v1/realtime?model=...`)\n206\t- `ag2client.js` already reads the model from the init config (`data.model`), so no client change needed\n207\t- Verify the model name is exactly what OpenAI expects (check API docs for `gpt-realtime-1.5` vs `gpt-4o-realtime-preview-2024-12-17` etc.)\n208\t\n209\t---\n210\t\n211\t## Change 3: Voice Change Tool\n212\t\n213\t### Design\n214\t\n215\tAdd a tool that the user can invoke via speech: *\"Switch to the ember voice\"* or *\"Change your voice to shimmer\"*\n216\t\n217\t**Challenge**: Changing voice requires creating a new OpenAI Realtime session with a different `voice` parameter. The current session must be torn down and a new one established, seamlessly.\n218\t\n219\t### Available OpenAI Voices\n220\t`alloy`, `ash`, `ballad`, `coral`, `echo`, `fable`, `nova`, `onyx`, `sage`, `shimmer`, `verse`\n221\t\n222\t### Implementation Strategy\n223\t\n224\t1. **Register a `change_voice` tool** with the realtime session\n225\t2. When the tool is called:\n226\t   a. Save the current conversation context (recent messages, system message)\n227\t   b. Generate a new ephemeral key with the requested voice\n228\t   c. Send a `ducke.reinit` message to the client with the new session config\n229\t   d. Client tears down old WebRTC peer connection and establishes a new one\n230\t   e. Inject saved context into the new session via `conversation.item.create` messages in the init chunks\n231\t3. The user hears DUCK-E respond in the new voice confirming the change\n232\t\n233\t### Files to Modify\n234\t\n235\t| File | Change |\n236\t|------|--------|\n237\t| `app/realtime_session.py` | Add `change_voice()` method, track conversation context |\n238\t| `app/main.py` | Register `change_voice` tool |\n239\t| `app/website_files/static/ag2client.js` | Handle `ducke.reinit` message — tear down and reconnect WebRTC |\n240\t| `app/website_files/static/main.js` | Show voice change status in transcript |\n241\t\n242\t### Context Preservation Details\n243\t\n244\tWhen switching voices:\n245\t1. Collect the last N conversation items (system message + recent turns) from the transcript\n246\t2. These become `init` chunks in the new session's `ducke.reinit` message:\n247\t   ```json\n248\t   {\n249\t     \"type\": \"ducke.reinit\",\n250\t     \"config\": { /* new ephemeral key config */ },\n251\t     \"init\": [\n252\t       {\"type\": \"conversation.item.create\", \"item\": {\"type\": \"message\", \"role\": \"system\", \"content\": [{\"type\": \"input_text\", \"text\": \"...system message...\"}]}},\n253\t       {\"type\": \"conversation.item.create\", \"item\": {\"type\": \"message\", \"role\": \"user\", \"content\": [{\"type\": \"input_text\", \"text\": \"...prior user message...\"}]}},\n254\t       {\"type\": \"conversation.item.create\", \"item\": {\"type\": \"message\", \"role\": \"assistant\", \"content\": [{\"type\": \"input_text\", \"text\": \"...prior assistant response...\"}]}}\n255\t     ]\n256\t   }\n257\t   ```\n258\t3. The client replays these into the new data channel after the new session is established\n259\t\n260\t### Voice Change Tool Definition\n261\t\n262\t```python\n263\tsession.register_tool(\n264\t    name=\"change_voice\",\n265\t    description=\"Change the assistant's voice. Available voices: alloy, ash, ballad, coral, echo, fable, nova, onyx, sage, shimmer, verse\",\n266\t    handler=handle_voice_change,\n267\t    parameters={\n268\t        \"type\": \"object\",\n269\t        \"properties\": {\n270\t            \"voice\": {\n271\t                \"type\": \"string\",\n272\t                \"enum\": [\"alloy\", \"ash\", \"ballad\", \"coral\", \"echo\", \"fable\", \"nova\", \"onyx\", \"sage\", \"shimmer\", \"verse\"],\n273\t                \"description\": \"The voice to switch to\"\n274\t            }\n275\t        },\n276\t        \"required\": [\"voice\"]\n277\t    }\n278\t)\n279\t```\n280\t\n281\t---\n282\t\n283\t## Change 4: User Memory (Google OAuth)\n284\t\n285\t### Architecture\n286\t\n287\t```\n288\tBrowser ──(Google OAuth)──> Backend ──(headers: x-forwarded-user, x-user-email)──> WebSocket\n289\t                                          │\n290\t                                          ▼\n291\t                                   Memory Store (per-user)\n292\t```\n293\t\n294\t### Authentication Flow\n295\t\n296\tThe app sits behind a reverse proxy (e.g., oauth2-proxy, Tailscale with Google OIDC) that handles Google OAuth and injects headers. The backend already logs `x-forwarded-user` (see `main.py:214`).\n297\t\n298\t1. **No OAuth implementation in DUCK-E itself** — rely on the upstream proxy to authenticate and inject headers:\n299\t   - `x-forwarded-user` — Google user ID or email\n300\t   - `x-forwarded-email` — User's email\n301\t   - `x-forwarded-name` — Display name\n302\t2. Backend extracts user identity from these headers on WebSocket connect\n303\t3. Memory is keyed to the user identity\n304\t\n305\t### Memory Store Design\n306\t\n307\tUse a simple JSON file store (one file per user) for v1. Can be upgraded to Redis/SQLite later.\n308\t\n309\t```\n310\t/data/memory/\n311\t  user_sha256hash1.json\n312\t  user_sha256hash2.json\n313\t```\n314\t\n315\tEach file:\n316\t```json\n317\t{\n318\t  \"user_id\": \"user@example.com\",\n319\t  \"created_at\": \"2026-03-12T...\",\n320\t  \"updated_at\": \"2026-03-12T...\",\n321\t  \"facts\": [\n322\t    {\"text\": \"User prefers Celsius for weather\", \"created_at\": \"...\"},\n323\t    {\"text\": \"User's name is Alex\", \"created_at\": \"...\"}\n324\t  ]\n325\t}\n326\t```\n327\t\n328\t### Memory Tools\n329\t\n330\tRegister two tools with the realtime session:\n331\t\n332\t1. **`save_memory`** — Save a fact about the user for future reference\n333\t   - Called proactively by the model when it learns something worth remembering\n334\t   - Parameters: `{\"fact\": \"string\"}`\n335\t\n336\t2. **`recall_memories`** — Retrieve stored memories about the current user\n337\t   - Called at session start (injected into system message) and on-demand\n338\t   - Parameters: none\n339\t   - Returns: list of stored facts\n340\t\n341\t### System Message Enhancement\n342\t\n343\tOn session start, after identifying the user from headers:\n344\t```\n345\tYou are DUCK-E... [existing system message]\n346\t\n347\tThe current user is {user_name} ({user_email}).\n348\tHere are things you remember about this user:\n349\t- {fact1}\n350\t- {fact2}\n351\t...\n352\tUse save_memory when you learn preferences or important information about the user.\n353\t```\n354\t\n355\t### Files to Create/Modify\n356\t\n357\t| File | Change |\n358\t|------|--------|\n359\t| `app/memory.py` | **NEW** — `UserMemoryStore` class with load/save/add_fact/get_facts |\n360\t| `app/main.py` | Extract user from headers, load memories, inject into system message, register memory tools |\n361\t| `app/realtime_session.py` | Pass user context through |\n362\t\n363\t### Security\n364\t- Hash user emails before using as filenames to prevent path traversal\n365\t- Validate header values (already have input validation patterns)\n366\t- Memory file directory should be outside the app root\n367\t- Set a max facts limit per user (e.g., 100) to prevent abuse\n368\t\n369\t---\n370\t\n371\t## Change 5: Web Fetch Tool\n372\t\n373\t### Motivation\n374\t\n375\tThe existing `web_search` tool finds information via OpenAI's Responses API, but the user cannot ask DUCK-E to read a specific URL they already have. A `web_fetch` tool complements web search by retrieving and extracting readable content from a given URL — useful for summarizing articles, reading documentation, or pulling data from a known page.\n376\t\n377\t### Design\n378\t\n379\tRegister a `web_fetch` tool alongside the existing `web_search` tool. The user can say things like *\"Read this article for me: https://example.com/post\"* or *\"What does this page say?\"* and DUCK-E fetches the content, extracts the text, and summarizes it.\n380\t\n381\t### Implementation\n382\t\n383\t1. **Fetch** the URL using `httpx.AsyncClient` with a reasonable timeout (15s) and a browser-like `User-Agent`\n384\t2. **Extract text** from HTML using `beautifulsoup4` (`BeautifulSoup` with `html.parser`) — strip nav, script, style, and footer elements, then extract visible text\n385\t3. **Truncate** to 3000 characters to stay within realtime session context limits\n386\t4. **Validate** the URL for safety before fetching\n387\t\n388\t### URL Validation & Security\n389\t\n390\t- Only allow `http` and `https` schemes — reject `file://`, `ftp://`, `data:`, etc.\n391\t- Block private/internal IP ranges (`10.x`, `172.16-31.x`, `192.168.x`, `127.x`, `169.254.x`, `::1`, `fc00::/7`) to prevent SSRF\n392\t- Resolve the hostname before connecting and verify the resolved IP is not private\n393\t- Reject URLs longer than 2048 characters\n394\t- Follow redirects (up to 5) but re-validate each hop's resolved IP\n395\t- Set `Content-Type` accept header to prefer `text/html`\n396\t\n397\t### Input Validation\n398\t\n399\tAdd a `FetchUrl` validator in `app/models/validators.py` (alongside the existing `SearchQuery`):\n400\t- Validate URL format via `urllib.parse.urlparse`\n401\t- Enforce scheme whitelist (`http`, `https`)\n402\t- Strip fragments and authentication components (`user:pass@`)\n403\t- Block known-bad patterns (e.g., `localhost`, `0.0.0.0`)\n404\t\n405\t### Tool Definition\n406\t\n407\t```python\n408\tsession.register_tool(\n409\t    name=\"web_fetch\",\n410\t    description=\"Fetch and read the content of a web page at a given URL. Returns the extracted text content. Use this when the user provides a specific URL they want you to read or summarize.\",\n411\t    handler=web_fetch,\n412\t    parameters={\n413\t        \"type\": \"object\",\n414\t        \"properties\": {\n415\t            \"url\": {\n416\t                \"type\": \"string\",\n417\t                \"description\": \"The full URL to fetch (must be http or https)\"\n418\t            }\n419\t        },\n420\t        \"required\": [\"url\"]\n421\t    }\n422\t)\n423\t```\n424\t\n425\t### Handler Implementation\n426\t\n427\t```python\n428\tasync def web_fetch(url: Annotated[str, \"url\"]) -> str:\n429\t    validated = FetchUrl(url=url)\n430\t    safe_url = str(validated.url)\n431\t\n432\t    async with httpx.AsyncClient(\n433\t        timeout=15.0,\n434\t        follow_redirects=True,\n435\t        max_redirects=5,\n436\t        headers={\n437\t            \"User-Agent\": \"DUCK-E/1.0 (voice assistant; +https://github.com/jedarden/duck-e)\",\n438\t            \"Accept\": \"text/html,application/xhtml+xml,text/plain;q=0.9\",\n439\t        },\n440\t    ) as client:\n441\t        resp = await client.get(safe_url)\n442\t        resp.raise_for_status()\n443\t\n444\t    content_type = resp.headers.get(\"content-type\", \"\")\n445\t    if \"text/html\" in content_type:\n446\t        soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \"html.parser\")\n447\t        for tag in soup([\"script\", \"style\", \"nav\", \"footer\", \"header\", \"aside\"]):\n448\t            tag.decompose()\n449\t        text = soup.get_text(separator=\"\\n\", strip=True)\n450\t    elif \"text/plain\" in content_type or \"application/json\" in content_type:\n451\t        text = resp.text\n452\t    else:\n453\t        return f\"Unsupported content type: {content_type}\"\n454\t\n455\t    if len(text) > 3000:\n456\t        text = text[:3000] + \"\\n\\n[Content truncated — page had more text]\"\n457\t\n458\t    return text\n459\t```\n460\t\n461\t### Dependencies\n462\t\n463\tAdd `beautifulsoup4` to `requirements.txt`. `httpx` is already a dependency (used by `RealtimeSession`).\n464\t\n465\t### Cost Tracking\n466\t\n467\tWeb fetch calls should be tracked via the existing `cost_tracker` for observability, even though they don't consume OpenAI tokens directly. Log the URL, response size, and latency.\n468\t\n469\t### Files to Create/Modify\n470\t\n471\t| File | Change |\n472\t|------|--------|\n473\t| `requirements.txt` | Add `beautifulsoup4` |\n474\t| `app/main.py` | Add `web_fetch` handler function and register the tool with the session |\n475\t| `app/models/validators.py` | Add `FetchUrl` validator with URL scheme/IP validation |\n476\t\n477\t---\n478\t\n479\t## Change 6: Agentation Library Integration\n480\t\n481\t### What Agentation Does\n482\t\n483\tAgentation is a React-based UI annotation tool that lets users click on page elements to annotate them with CSS selectors, position data, and comments. It provides structured feedback for AI agents.\n484\t\n485\t### Integration Approach\n486\t\n487\tSince DUCK-E's frontend is vanilla JS (not React), we need to either:\n488\t\n489\t**Option A: Mount React for Agentation only** (recommended)\n490\t- Add React + ReactDOM via CDN\n491\t- Mount `<Agentation />` component into a dedicated div\n492\t- Configure callbacks to pipe annotations into the chat/voice context\n493\t\n494\t**Option B: Use Agentation's CSS-only variant**\n495\t- If available, use a framework-agnostic build\n496\t\n497\t### Implementation\n498\t\n499\t1. Add React 18 CDN scripts to `chat.html`\n500\t2. Add Agentation via CDN or bundle it\n501\t3. Create a mount point `<div id=\"agentation-root\"></div>` in the page\n502\t4. Initialize with callbacks:\n503\t\n504\t```html\n505\t<script src=\"https://unpkg.com/react@18/umd/react.production.min.js\"></script>\n506\t<script src=\"https://unpkg.com/react-dom@18/umd/react-dom.production.min.js\"></script>\n507\t<script src=\"https://unpkg.com/agentation/dist/index.umd.js\"></script>\n508\t<script>\n509\t  const agentationRoot = document.getElementById('agentation-root');\n510\t  const root = ReactDOM.createRoot(agentationRoot);\n511\t  root.render(\n512\t    React.createElement(Agentation.Agentation, {\n513\t      onAnnotationAdd: (annotation) => {\n514\t        // Send annotation context to DUCK-E via the data channel or display in transcript\n515\t        console.log('Annotation added:', annotation);\n516\t        addTranscriptMessage('system', `Annotation on \"${annotation.element}\": ${annotation.comment}`);\n517\t      },\n518\t      onSubmit: (output, annotations) => {\n519\t        // Pipe structured feedback to the voice session\n520\t        console.log('Feedback submitted:', output);\n521\t      },\n522\t      copyToClipboard: true\n523\t    })\n524\t  );\n525\t</script>\n526\t```\n527\t\n528\t### Files to Modify\n529\t\n530\t| File | Change |\n531\t|------|--------|\n532\t| `app/website_files/templates/chat.html` | Add React CDN, Agentation script, mount point div |\n533\t| `app/website_files/static/main.js` | Add handlers for annotation events |\n534\t| `app/middleware/security.py` | Update CSP to allow React/Agentation CDN sources |\n535\t| `package.json` | Optionally add `agentation` as dependency for bundling |\n536\t\n537\t---\n538\t\n539\t## Change 7: Footer/Version Pushed Below Fold\n540\t\n541\t### Current Behavior\n542\t\n543\tThe footer with version badge and GitHub link is always visible at the bottom of the viewport. The chat transcript is in a fixed-height card.\n544\t\n545\t### Desired Behavior\n546\t\n547\t- Footer stays in document flow (not fixed)\n548\t- As chat history grows, the transcript area expands\n549\t- The footer gets pushed down naturally, eventually below the fold\n550\t- User can scroll down to see it, but it doesn't consume screen real estate during active chat\n551\t\n552\t### Implementation\n553\t\n554\t1. Remove `min-height: 100vh` constraint from container or make it `height: auto`\n555\t2. Change transcript card from fixed height to `flex-grow: 1` with no max-height\n556\t3. Footer remains in normal flow — as content grows, it scrolls away\n557\t4. On initial load (no chat), footer is visible at bottom of viewport\n558\t\n559\t### CSS Changes\n560\t\n561\t```css\n562\t/* Container: use min-height instead of fixed height */\n563\t.container {\n564\t    min-height: 100vh;\n565\t    display: flex;\n566\t    flex-direction: column;\n567\t}\n568\t\n569\t/* Main content area: grows to fill space */\n570\t.main-content {\n571\t    flex: 1;\n572\t    display: flex;\n573\t    flex-direction: column;\n574\t}\n575\t\n576\t/* Transcript: grows with content, no max-height cap */\n577\t.main-content.has-history .transcript-card {\n578\t    flex: 1;\n579\t    max-height: none; /* Remove any max-height */\n580\t    overflow-y: auto;\n581\t}\n582\t\n583\t/* Footer: stays in flow, pushed down by content */\n584\t.footer {\n585\t    flex-shrink: 0;\n586\t    /* Remove any position: fixed/sticky */\n587\t}\n588\t```\n589\t\n590\t### Files to Modify\n591\t\n592\t| File | Change |\n593\t|------|--------|\n594\t| `app/website_files/templates/chat.html` | Update CSS for container, transcript card, and footer layout |\n595\t\n596\t---\n597\t\n598\t## Change 8: Tool Call Display in Chat + Button Design Consistency\n599\t\n600\t### Tool Call Display\n601\t\n602\tWhen DUCK-E makes a tool call (weather, web search, voice change, memory), show it in the chat transcript as a collapsible card.\n603\t\n604\t#### Design\n605\t\n606\t```\n607\t┌─────────────────────────────────────┐\n608\t│ 🔧 get_current_weather              │  ← Collapsed (default)\n609\t│    ▸ Click to expand                │\n610\t└─────────────────────────────────────┘\n611\t\n612\t┌─────────────────────────────────────┐\n613\t│ 🔧 get_current_weather              │  ← Expanded\n614\t│    ▾ Click to collapse              │\n615\t│ ┌─────────────────────────────────┐ │\n616\t│ │ location: \"San Francisco\"      │ │\n617\t│ │ timestamp: 2026-03-12T14:30    │ │\n618\t│ │ status: completed              │ │\n619\t│ │ result: {\"temp_f\": 62, ...}    │ │\n620\t│ └─────────────────────────────────┘ │\n621\t└─────────────────────────────────────┘\n622\t```\n623\t\n624\t#### Implementation\n625\t\n626\t1. Intercept `response.function_call_arguments.done` and `response.output_item.done` events in `main.js`\n627\t2. Add a new message type `tool_call` to the transcript system\n628\t3. Render tool call messages with a collapsible details/summary HTML element\n629\t\n630\t```javascript\n631\t// New function in main.js\n632\tconst addToolCallMessage = (name, args, callId) => {\n633\t  transcriptMessages.push({\n634\t    role: 'tool',\n635\t    type: 'tool_call',\n636\t    toolName: name,\n637\t    toolArgs: args,\n638\t    callId: callId,\n639\t    status: 'pending',\n640\t    result: null,\n641\t    timestamp: Date.now()\n642\t  });\n643\t  renderTranscript();\n644\t  showTranscript();\n645\t};\n646\t\n647\t// In renderTranscript, handle tool_call type:\n648\tif (msg.type === 'tool_call') {\n649\t  return `\n650\t    <div class=\"transcript-message tool-call\" data-idx=\"${idx}\">\n651\t      <details class=\"tool-call-details\">\n652\t        <summary class=\"tool-call-summary\">\n653\t          <span class=\"tool-call-icon\">🔧</span>\n654\t          <span class=\"tool-call-name\">${msg.toolName}</span>\n655\t          <span class=\"tool-call-status ${msg.status}\">${msg.status}</span>\n656\t        </summary>\n657\t        <div class=\"tool-call-metadata\">\n658\t          <pre>${JSON.stringify(JSON.parse(msg.toolArgs), null, 2)}</pre>\n659\t          ${msg.result ? `<div class=\"tool-call-result\"><strong>Result:</strong><pre>${msg.result}</pre></div>` : ''}\n660\t        </div>\n661\t      </details>\n662\t    </div>\n663\t  `;\n664\t}\n665\t```\n666\t\n667\t### Button Design Consistency\n668\t\n669\tCurrently the controls use a mix of styles:\n670\t- Connect/Disconnect button: `audio-btn` class\n671\t- var(--bg-secondary);\n690\t    color: var(--text-primary);\n691\t    font-family: inherit;\n692\t    font-size: 14px;\n693\t    font-weight: 500;\n694\t    cursor: pointer;\n695\t    transition: all 0.2s ease;\n696\t}\n697\t\n698\t.ducke-btn:hover {\n699\t    background: var(--bg-tertiary);\n700\t    border-color: var(--primary-light);\n701\t}\n702\t\n703\t/* Variants */\n704\t.ducke-btn--primary {\n705\t    background: var(--primary);\n706\t    border-color: var(--primary);\n707\t}\n708\t\n709\t.ducke-btn--primary:hover {\n710\t    background: var(--primary-dark);\n711\t}\n712\t\n713\t.ducke-btn--danger {\n714\t    /* For disconnect state */\n715\t    background: rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.1);\n716\t    border-color: var(--danger);\n717\t    color: var(--danger);\n718\t}\n719\t\n720\t/* Sizes */\n721\t.ducke-btn--sm {\n722\t    padding: 6px 12px;\n723\t    font-size: 12px;\n724\t}\n725\t\n726\t/* Icon-only */\n727\t.ducke-btn--icon {\n728\t    padding: 10px;\n729\t    border-radius: 50%;\n730\t}\n731\t```\n732\t\n733\tApply this system to all interactive elements: Connect, Disconnect, Mute, PTT toggle, PTT hold, Clear |\n742\t\n743\t---\n744\t\n745\t## Change 9: Estimated Hourly Cost Display\n746\t\n747\t### gpt-realtime-1.5 Pricing\n748\t\n749\t| Token Type | Input (per 1M) | Cached Input (per 1M) | Output (per 1M) |\n750\t|------------|----------------|----------------------|-----------------|\n751\t| **Text** | $4.00 | $0.40 | $16.00 |\n752\t| **Audio** | $32.00 | $0.40 | $64.00 |\n753\t| **Image** | $5.00 | $0.50 | N/A |\n754\t\n755\tFor a voice assistant, the dominant costs are **audio tokens**:\n756\t- Audio input: $32.00 / 1M tokens\n757\t- Audio output: $64.00 / 1M tokens\n758\t\n759\t### Cost Estimation Model\n760\t\n761\tOpenAI's Realtime API uses audio tokens at roughly **50 tokens per second** of audio (based on the 24kHz PCM encoding and OpenAI's tokenization). Estimating for a typical voice conversation:\n762\t\n763\t| Scenario | Audio In (tokens/hr) | Audio Out (tokens/hr) | Text In (tokens/hr) | Text Out (tokens/hr) | Estimated Cost/hr |\n764\t|----------|---------------------|----------------------|--------------------|--------------------|-------------------|\n765\t| **Light** (user talks 5 min/hr, DUCK-E responds 5 min/hr) | 15,000 | 15,000 | ~2,000 | ~2,000 | ~$1.48 |\n766\t| **Moderate** (user talks 15 min/hr, DUCK-E responds 15 min/hr) | 45,000 | 45,000 | ~5,000 | ~5,000 | ~$4.42 |\n767\t| **Heavy** (user talks 25 min/hr, DUCK-E responds 25 min/hr) | 75,000 | 75,000 | ~10,000 | ~10,000 | ~$7.36 |\n768\t\n769\tFormula:\n770\t```\n771\tcost_per_hour = (audio_in_tokens * $32/1M) + (audio_out_tokens * $64/1M)\n772\t             + (text_in_tokens * $4/1M) + (text_out_tokens * $16/1M)\n773\t```\n774\t\n775\tNote: The existing `CostProtectionMiddleware` tracks session costs server-side but doesn't expose them to the user.\n776\t\n777\t### Implementation\n778\t\n779\tEvery `response.done` event from the Realtime API includes a `usage` object with token counts:\n780\t```json\n781\t{\n782\t  \"type\": \"response.done\",\n783\t  \"response\": {\n784\t    \"usage\": {\n785\t      \"total_tokens\": 1234,\n786\t      \"input_tokens\": 500,\n787\t      \"output_tokens\": 734,\n788\t      \"input_token_details\": {\n789\t        \"text_tokens\": 100,\n790\t        \"audio_tokens\": 400,\n791\t        \"cached_tokens\": 50\n792\t      },\n793\t      \"output_token_details\": {\n794\t        \"text_tokens\": 134,\n795\t        \"audio_tokens\": 600\n796\t      }\n797\t    }\n798\t  }\n799\t}\n800\t```\n801\t\n802\tAccumulate these counts from each `response.done` in the frontend, apply the pricing rates, and derive the hourly estimate from `(total_cost / session_elapsed_hours)`.\n803\t\n804\t### UI Design\n805\t\n806\t#### Collapsed (default)\n807\t\n808\t```\n809\t┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐\n810\t│ ● Connected - DUCK-E is listening        │\n811\t│ Est. ~$3.20/hr  ▸                        │\n812\t└──────────────────────────────────────────┘\n813\t```\n814\t\n815\t#### Expanded (click to toggle)\n816\t\n817\t```\n818\t┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐\n819\t│ ● Connected - DUCK-E is listening        │\n820\t│ Est. ~$3.20/hr  ▾                        │\n821\t│ ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐ │\n822\t│ │ Session Duration   12m 34s           │ │\n823\t│ │ ─────────────────────────────────    │ │\n824\t│ │ Audio Input        $0.38             │ │\n825\t│ │ Audio Output       $0.72             │ │\n826\t│ │ Text Input         $0.01             │ │\n827\t│ │ Text Output        $0.04             │ │\n828\t│ │ Cached Input       $0.00             │ │\n829\t│ │ ─────────────────────────────────    │ │\n830\t│ │ Session Total      $1.15             │ │\n831\t│ └──────────────────────────────────────┘ │\n832\t└──────────────────────────────────────────┘\n833\t```\n834\t\n835\tThe cost display should:\n836\t- Only appear after the first `response.done` with usage data\n837\t- Update after each response\n838\t- Show estimated hourly rate in the collapsed view\n839\t- On click, expand to show per-category cost breakdown and session duration\n840\t- Use a muted color to not distract from the conversation\n841\t- Flash briefly when updated\n842\t- Use `<details>/<summary>` for the expand/collapse (consistent with tool call cards from Change 7)\n843\t\n844\t#### Frontend Implementation\n845\t\n846\t```javascript\n847\t// Cost tracking state\n848\tlet sessionCost = {\n849\t  startTime: null,\n850\t  totalInputTextTokens: 0,\n851\t  totalInputAudioTokens: 0,\n852\t  totalOutputTextTokens: 0,\n853\t  totalOutputAudioTokens: 0,\n854\t  totalCachedTokens: 0,\n855\t};\n856\t\n857\t// Pricing constants (gpt-realtime-1.5)\n858\tconst PRICING = {\n859\t  textInput: 4.00 / 1_000_000,\n860\t  textOutput: 16.00 / 1_000_000,\n861\t  audioInput: 32.00 / 1_000_000,\n862\t  audioOutput: 64.00 / 1_000_000,\n863\t  cachedInput: 0.40 / 1_000_000,\n864\t};\n865\t\n866\tconst updateCostFromResponse = (usage) => {\n867\t  if (!sessionCost.startTime) sessionCost.startTime = Date.now();\n868\t\n869\t  const details = usage.input_token_details || {};\n870\t  const outDetails = usage.output_token_details || {};\n871\t\n872\t  sessionCost.totalInputTextTokens += details.text_tokens || 0;\n873\t  sessionCost.totalInputAudioTokens += details.audio_tokens || 0;\n874\t  sessionCost.totalCachedTokens += details.cached_tokens || 0;\n875\t  sessionCost.totalOutputTextTokens += outDetails.text_tokens || 0;\n876\t  sessionCost.totalOutputAudioTokens += outDetails.audio_tokens || 0;\n877\t\n878\t  const totalCost =\n879\t    (sessionCost.totalInputTextTokens * PRICING.textInput) +\n880\t    (sessionCost.totalInputAudioTokens * PRICING.audioInput) +\n881\t    (sessionCost.totalOutputTextTokens * PRICING.textOutput) +\n882\t    (sessionCost.totalOutputAudioTokens * PRICING.audioOutput) +\n883\t    (sessionCost.totalCachedTokens * PRICING.cachedInput);\n884\t\n885\t  const elapsedHours = (Date.now() - sessionCost.startTime) / 3_600_000;\n886\t  const hourlyRate = elapsedHours > 0 ? totalCost / elapsedHours : 0;\n887\t\n888\t  // Per-category costs for breakdown\n889\t  const costs = {\n890\t    audioInput:  sessionCost.totalInputAudioTokens  * PRICING.audioInput,\n891\t    audioOutput: sessionCost.totalOutputAudioTokens * PRICING.audioOutput,\n892\t    textInput:   sessionCost.totalInputTextTokens   * PRICING.textInput,\n893\t    textOutput:  sessionCost.totalOutputTextTokens  * PRICING.textOutput,\n894\t    cached:      sessionCost.totalCachedTokens      * PRICING.cachedInput,\n895\t  };\n896\t\n897\t  const elapsedMs = Date.now() - sessionCost.startTime;\n898\t  updateCostDisplay(totalCost, hourlyRate, costs, elapsedMs);\n899\t};\n900\t\n901\tconst updateCostDisplay = (totalCost, hourlyRate, costs, elapsedMs) => {\n902\t  const el = document.getElementById('cost-display');\n903\t  if (!el) return;\n904\t  el.style.display = 'block';\n905\t\n906\t  const fmt = (v) => '$' + v.toFixed(2);\n907\t  const mins = Math.floor(elapsedMs / 60000);\n908\t  const secs = Math.floor((elapsedMs % 60000) / 1000);\n909\t  const duration = `${mins}m ${secs.toString().padStart(2, '0')}s`;\n910\t\n911\t  el.innerHTML = `\n912\t    <details class=\"cost-details\">\n913\t      <summary class=\"cost-summary\">\n914\t        Est. ~${fmt(hourlyRate)}/hr\n915\t      </summary>\n916\t      <div class=\"cost-breakdown\">\n917\t        <div class=\"cost-row\"><span>Session Duration</span><span>${duration}</span></div>\n918\t        <hr class=\"cost-divider\">\n919\t        <div class=\"cost-row\"><span>Audio Input</span><span>${fmt(costs.audioInput)}</span></div>\n920\t        <div class=\"cost-row\"><span>Audio Output</span><span>${fmt(costs.audioOutput)}</span></div>\n921\t        <div class=\"cost-row\"><span>Text Input</span><span>${fmt(costs.textInput)}</span></div>\n922\t        <div class=\"cost-row\"><span>Text Output</span><span>${fmt(costs.textOutput)}</span></div>\n923\t        <div class=\"cost-row\"><span>Cached Input</span><span>${fmt(costs.cached)}</span></div>\n924\t        <hr class=\"cost-divider\">\n925\t        <div class=\"cost-row cost-total\"><span>Session Total</span><span>${fmt(totalCost)}</span></div>\n926\t      </div>\n927\t    </details>\n928\t  `;\n929\t};\n930\t\n931\t// In handleWebRTCMessage, add:\n932\tif (data.type === 'response.done' && data.response?.usage) {\n933\t  updateCostFromResponse(data.response.usage);\n934\t}\n935\t```\n936\t\n937\t### Files to Modify\n938\t\n939\t| File | Change |\n940\t|------|--------|\n941\t| `app/website_files/static/main.js` | Add cost tracking state, `updateCostFromResponse()`, intercept `response.done` events |\n942\t| `app/website_files/templates/chat.html` | Add cost display element near status indicator, CSS for cost badge |\n943\t| `app/website_files/static/ag2client.js` | Ensure `response.done` events are forwarded via `onMessage` (already done — all events are forwarded) |\n944\t\n945\t### Security Note\n946\t\n947\tCost data is computed entirely client-side from usage metadata in API responses. No API keys or billing credentials are exposed. The server-side `CostProtectionMiddleware` remains the authoritative cost limiter — this frontend display is informational only.\n948\t\n949\t---\n950\t\n951\t## Execution Order\n952\t\n953\tThe changes have dependencies and should be implemented in this order:\n954\t\n955\t```\n956\tPhase 1 — Foundation (no visible changes yet)\n957\t  1. Change 1: Remove AG2 → create RealtimeSession\n958\t  2. Change 2: Switch to gpt-realtime-1.5\n959\t\n960\tPhase 2 — Backend Features\n961\t  3. Change 4: Memory system (needs RealtimeSession for tool registration)\n962\t  4. Change 3: Voice change tool (needs RealtimeSession + reinit protocol)\n963\t  5. Change 5: Web fetch tool (needs RealtimeSession; complements existing web_search)\n964\t\n965\tPhase 3 — Frontend\n966\t  6. Change 8: Tool call display + button consistency\n967\t  7. Change 9: Cost display (depends on Change 8 for consistent UI patterns)\n968\t  8. Change 7: Footer/layout changes\n969\t  9. Change 6: Agentation integration\n970\t```\n971\t\n972\t### Risk Notes\n973\t\n974\t- **Change 1** is the riskiest — it replaces the core session management. Must verify the exact WebSocket message protocol AG2's RealtimeAgent uses by tracing actual messages.\n975\t- **Change 3** requires client-side reconnection logic, which is complex. The WebRTC peer connection teardown/rebuild needs careful handling of audio state.\n976\t- **Change 5** (web fetch) introduces SSRF risk if URL validation is incomplete. The IP resolution check before connecting is critical — must validate resolved IPs on every redirect hop, not just the initial hostname.\n977\t- **Change 6** introduces React as a dependency for a single component. If Agentation's UMD bundle size is too large, consider lazy-loading it.\n978\t- **Change 2** depends on `gpt-realtime-1.5` being a valid model identifier at OpenAI.
